# Ticket board вҖ” step 2 (proving Theorem 1.2 from the axioms)

Source of truth for the proof phase.  Rationale, DAG, conventions, and wave schedule:
[`step2-plan.md`](step2-plan.md).  The **step-1 board** (statement formalization, ticket IDs
`T-xx` cited in module docstrings) is archived at [`tickets-step1.md`](tickets-step1.md).
Difficulty: вӯҗ easy В· вӯҗвӯҗ medium В· вӯҗвӯҗвӯҗ hard/design-sensitive.  Model: **F** = Fable
(design-heavy), **O** = Opus (well-specified).  Status: вҳҗ open В· в—җ in progress В· вҳ‘ done.

Rules: **no new `axiom`s without explicit user approval** (census at 13 вҖ” B10 added by explicit decision, P-06 escalation; B9 base-generalized + B11 added by explicit decision, P-15 escalation, user-approved 2026-07-03; **B11 split into B11a `hilbertSymbol_normCriterion_finiteDyadic` + B11b `unramifiedQuadratic_units_are_norms` by P-23, census 12вҶ’13, user-approved 2026-07-04** вҖ” `dyadicNormCriterion` kept as a same-name theorem, spectral-norm bridge isolated as a `def IsUnramifiedQuadraticSpectral`, not an axiom); statement tickets add their sorried theorems to
`SORRY_ALLOWLIST` in `scripts/check_axioms.sh` (same commit, entry cites the ticket), proof
tickets remove them; every ticket's new theorems satisfy `#print axioms` вҠҶ std-3 вҲӘ the ticket's
**Ax** column; `GQ2/Foundations/Axioms.lean` is frozen; sessions claim a ticket by marking its
row в—җ before starting.  Paper: `paper/A_Profinite_Presentation_for_G__Q_2.pdf`.

every `t^k вү  1` has zero fixed space (**`fixedPoints_zpowers_tame_eq_zero`** вҖ” generalizes `fixedPoints_tame_inertia_eq_zero`: conjugates of `t^k` are powers of `t^k`, `вҠӨ` killed by `hfaith` instead of `hram`), so the geometric sum vanishes (**`sum_range_orderOf_smul_eq_zero`**), and for `Пү`-fixed `v` the transversal sum `w := ОЈ_{k вү  0, k.val < (qk).val} u^{k.val}вҖўv` (val-comparison picks one element of each pair `{k, qk}` вҖ” canonical, no choice, no induction) satisfies `w + ПүвҖўw = ОЈ_{kвү 0} u^{k.val}вҖўv = v`; so `ker(1+Пү) вҠҶ range(1+Пү)` and `#V^Пү ^2 вүӨ #kerВ·#range = #V` by first-iso counting (`AddSubgroup.card_eq_card_quotient_mul_card_addSubgroup` + `QuotientAddGroup.quotientKerEquivRange`).  **Statement amendment (documented)**: `involution_fixedPoints_sq_le` gained `hs1 : 1 вүӨ s` вҖ” the leaf was FALSE as previously stated for `s = 0` (`Пү = gвӮҖ^0 = 1`; (в—җ-history: **REDUCED TO THE WEIGHT-ORBIT KERNEL** (Fable, 2026-07-06, `GQ2/RegularSummand.lean`; library green 8671, census 15).  **Landed, sorry-free, std-3 / Ax вҲ…:** **`regular_summand_of_subgroup_summand`** вҖ” the paper's "Sylow criterion" as a concrete odd-index **relative trace**: a `P`-equivariant split pair `(j, q)` into a regular `рқ”ҪвӮӮ[P]`-module with `Odd P.index` yields the `C`-level pair, via `О№ v n g := j (gвҒ»В№ вҖў v) n 1` and `ПҒ F := вҲ‘б¶ _{gP вҲҲ C/P} g вҖў q (F(gВ·вҖ”))` (coset summand well-defined by `Quotient.lift` + `q`-equivariance; `ПҒвҲҳО№ = [C:P] вҖў id = id` by odd index + 2-torsion; equivariance by reindexing `C в§ё P` along `x вҶҰ hвҒ»В№ вҖў x`).  No induced-module formalism вҖ” all function-level.  **`lemma_6_11` is now ASSEMBLED** (Sylow 2-subgroup + `Sylow.not_dvd_index` odd index + the trace): its `sorryAx` enters only through the isolated kernel **`sylow_split_pair_of_ramified`** (new sorried statement)  **Kernel re-posed (Opus, same day):** the sole remaining sorry is now the clean, standard statement **`sylow_free_of_ramified`** вҖ” *`V\|_P` is equivariantly `вүғ+` a regular module `рқ”ҪвӮӮ[P]^r`*, i.e. free of rank `r` over `рқ”ҪвӮӮ[P]`; `sylow_split_pair_of_ramified` is now **proved from it** (`j := ПҶ`, `q := ПҶвҒ»В№`, retraction-equivariance by `ПҶ`-injectivity, `qвҲҳj=id` by `symm_apply_apply`). Fully constructive, ~620 new lines, no `рқ”ҪМ„вӮӮ`, no structure theorem, no finiteness in the splitting: `ОҪ := Оі+1` has `ОҪ^{2^s} = 0` and group-sum `= ОҪ^{2^sвҲ’1}` (squaring induction, no Lucas); given a full-depth `vвӮҖ`, a functional `О»` with `О»(ОҪ^{2^sвҲ’1}vвӮҖ)=1` makes `T := ПҶвҲҳj` (coefficient map вҲҳ orbit map) `= 1 + (Ој+1)B` with `(Ој+1)^{2^s}=0` вҹ№ **explicit geometric-series inverse** вҹ№ `ПҒ := TвҒ»В№вҲҳПҶ` retracts `j`, one regular block splits equivariantly, recurse (bound inherited); no full-depth vector вҹ№ kernel-filtration bound collapses `V = 0`.  **`sylow_free_of_ramified` is now PROVED** from it (cyclic Sylow toolbox + tame relation transported along `c`); the residual sorry is the pure **counting inequality `card_fixedPoints_pow_le_of_ramified`** (`#V^P ^ |P| вүӨ #V` on a ramified simple faithful module) вҖ” no вҲғ-iso content left.  Paper cross-checked (pp. 29вҖ“30 read this session): the criterion replaces the two Lean-hostile steps (Clifford induction over `рқ”ҪМ„вӮӮ`; faithfully-flat projectivity descent) by their rational counting shadow.  рқ”ҪвӮӮ-rational plan for the inequality banked in the file section docstring: Г©tale `рқ”ҪвӮӮ[вҹЁП„вҹ©]` factor fields + single-`C`-orbit faithfulness (cyclic `вҹЁП„вҹ©` has characteristic subgroups) + the OвӮӮ-linchpin (a `P`-stabilizer element acting `K`-linearly centralizes `вҹЁП„вҹ©` вҹ№ abelian normal closure вҹ№ nontrivial normal 2-subgroup вҹ№ `FoxH.lemma_5_12` vs faithfulness) + finite-field semilinear fixed-point descent (additive Hilbert 90 / normal basis) вҖ” a recorded deviation from the paper (which uses 1-dimensional `рқ”ҪМ„вӮӮ`-weight lines); de-risks the remainder from 'Clifford over `рқ”ҪМ„вӮӮ`, poor Mathlib support' to explicit finite-field linear algebra.  New gotchas banked: numeral `rw` motive failure at `(2 : Module.End (ZMod 2) M)` (the polymorphic `one_add_one_eq_two` pattern catches the `2` in `ZMod 2`'s instance chain вҖ” pin with an explicitly-typed `have` first); `Fin.cons` on a constant family needs `(Оұ := fun _ => M)` everywhere; a single `rw [AddEquiv.apply_symm_apply]` rewrites all identical occurrences (a second copy errors).  **Reduced to the involution (Opus, 2026-07-06, std-3, Ax вҲ… for the reduction): `card_fixedPoints_pow_le_of_half` + Jordan-increment concavity land.**  The counting bound `card_fixedPoints_pow_le_of_ramified` is now PROVED from a strictly smaller leaf `involution_fixedPoints_sq_le` (`#V^Пү ^ 2 вүӨ #V` for the involution `Пү = gвӮҖ^{2^{s-1}}` of the cyclic Sylow-2), via the standard elementary-abelian / Chouinard reduction, all constructive: **`finrank_ker_pow_succ`** (`dim ker ОҪ^{k+1} = dim ker ОҪ^k + dim(im ОҪ^k вҠ“ ker ОҪ)`, rank-nullity for `ОҪ^k : ker ОҪ^{k+1} вҶ’ im ОҪ^k вҠ“ ker ОҪ`) вҮ’ **`finrank_ker_pow_concave`** (the increment `dim(im ОҪ^k вҠ“ ker ОҪ)` is antitone by `finrank_mono` on `im ОҪ^{k+1} вүӨ im ОҪ^k`); two `в„•`-lemmas **`seq_double_le`** (concavity's automatic `b(2m) вүӨ 2 b m`) and **`seq_first_increment_le`** (two equal `m`-term antitone sums are termwise equal вҮ’ all increments flatten, `Finset.sum_eq_sum_iff_of_le` + squeeze); and **`card_fixedPoints_pow_le_of_half`** wiring them to `b k := dim ker(nuOp gвӮҖ)^k` with the cardвҶ”finrank bridge (`Module.card_eq_pow_finrank`, `ZMod.card`), `b(2^s) = dim V` (`nuOp_pow_card_eq_zero`), the freshman `nuOp(gвӮҖ^{2^t}) = (nuOp gвӮҖ)^{2^t}` (`genOp_pow` + `add_pow_two_pow_of_two_eq_zero`), and the Пү-fixed-points вҶ” `ker` count.  So `#V^Пү ^ 2 вүӨ #V` (the involution) + concavity force `2^sВ·dim V^P = dim V`, i.e. the full bound.  `#print axioms`: the reduction is Ax вҲ…; `sorryAx` enters `lemma_6_11` only through `involution_fixedPoints_sq_le`.  **The residual leaf is now the single-involution case** вҖ” quadratic descent (additive Hilbert 90) rather than a cyclic-group weight-orbit analysis; a much smaller finite-field-linear-algebra target. ## Per-ticket acceptance criteria

Common to all: `lake build GQ2` green; `scripts/check_axioms.sh` green (allowlist edits per the
rules above); `#print axioms` of every new theorem вҠҶ std-3 вҲӘ the **Ax** column; docstrings carry
paper eq./В§ cross-references; new files, own board row only.

- **P-01** вҳ‘: `docs/STATUS.md` regenerated to the current tree (it stops at 2026-07-02); a script or
  Lean file (`scripts/axiom_ledger.*` or `GQ2/AxiomLedger.lean`) that reports, for every theorem in
  `GQ2`, its non-std-3 axioms, diffable against the per-ticket **Ax** declarations.  Re-run
  instructions in the file header.
  *Done.* `GQ2/AxiomLedger.lean` вҖ” a `run_cmd` metaprogram over the elaborated environment
  (`Lean.collectAxioms` per decl; robust to `namespace`/`private`, which the shell
  `.claude/tools/lean4/check_axioms.sh` cannot see).  Re-run: `lake env lean GQ2/AxiomLedger.lean`
  (header documents it; **not** imported by `GQ2.lean`, so `lake build GQ2` never runs it).  Output:
  per-B-axiom consumer lists (diff vs App. D В§C), the `sorryAx` gap map, and an **ALARM** count for
  any other non-standard axiom.  Current run: 613 tracked decls, 601 at std-3, ALARM 0; only B7 has
  consumers (its 6 Euler stress tests), gap map = 6 (the 3 root sorries + 3 transitive).
  `docs/STATUS.md` rewritten as a per-layer ledger (axiom layer, 3-sorry gap map, def-layers
  T-05вҖҰT-18, proved infra), with verify-from-scratch commands.
- **P-02** вҳ‘: sorry replaced; **zero sorries in `Reconstruction.lean`**, allowlist entry removed,
  `exists_contSurj_of_card_le`/`reconstruction_of_equinum`/`reconstruction` all `#print axioms` =
  std-3 (`lean_verify`'d), `check_axioms.sh` green (census 10).  Level sets nonempty+finite via
  `contSurj_quotient_nonempty_finite`; the compatible family via `konigFunctor : OpenNormalSubgroup
  (ProfiniteGrp.of R) вҘӨ Type` + `nonempty_sections_of_finite_cofiltered_system` (KГ¶nig), as the
  recipe said.  **Deviation from the recipe's assembly step**: instead of building a cone over
  `ProfiniteGrp.diagram R` and `isLimitCone.lift`, the section is assembled by an **elementary**
  embedding `e : R вҶӘ вҲҸ_U R/U` (closed embedding, `R` compact/`Q` Hausdorff) + **two Cantor
  intersections** (`IsCompact.nonempty_iInter_of_directed_nonempty_isCompact_isClosed`): one in `R`
  realizes each compatible family as `e r` (вҮ’ `ПҲ := eвҒ»В№вҲҳОҰ` a continuous hom), one in `S` gives `ПҲ`
  surjective.  **Why**: the `ProfiniteGrp.diagram` objects carry the discrete `вҠҘ` topology, not
  `R/U`'s coinduced (equal but not defeq) topology, and `(diagram R).obj U` won't even synthesize a
  `TopologicalSpace` when used as a bare `ContinuousMonoidHom` codomain вҖ” so the categorical
  cone/lift route fights Mathlib's `CompHausLike`/`FiniteGrp` coercions at every step.  The
  product-embedding route stays in natural quotient topologies throughout.  Reusable spinoffs (top
  of the file, `open CategoryTheory`): `projMap`(+`_mk`/`_surjective`/`_id`/`_comp_apply`) and
  `konigFunctor` вҖ” for **P-04/P-05** (also over `OpenNormalSubgroup (ProfiniteGrp.of _)`).
- **P-03**: `FreeProfiniteGroup X` is t.f.g. for finite `X` (the generators' images topologically
  generate вҖ” density of the free group in its completion); t.f.g. passes to `profiniteQuotient`;
  instantiate: `GammaA` t.f.g. in the exact `вҲғ s : Finset _, вҖҰ` form `main_presentation` consumes.
  *Done (`GQ2/FinitelyGenerated.lean`, std-3):* predicate `IsTopologicallyFinGen G` (unfolds to the
  raw `main_presentation` form); `IsTopologicallyFinGen.of_surjective` (transfer along a continuous
  surjection вҖ” `DenseRange.topologicalClosure_map_subgroup`); `isTopologicallyFinGen_freeProfiniteGroup`
  (finite `X` вҖ” `ProfiniteGrp.ProfiniteCompletion.denseRange` + `FreeGroup.closure_range_of`);
  `gammaA_isTopologicallyFinGen` + `gammaA_topologicallyFinitelyGenerated` (the raw `вҲғ`-form P-19 feeds
  to `main_presentation`).
- **P-04** вҳ‘: (i) `tameRelator`/`wildRelator` of `univMarking` lie in `NA` (each dies in every
  admissible quotient вҖ” `map_*Relator_eq_one_iff` + `IsAdmissibleU`); (ii) the closed normal
  closure of `{xвӮҖ, xвӮҒ}`-images in `О“_A` is pro-2 (`IsProP 2`, via `MaxProP.lean`'s
  characterization: every open normal subgroup of `О“_A` pulls back to an admissible-dominated one вҖ”
  the Lemma 2.1 subdirect-closure argument).  Design note documenting the limit argument.
  *Done (`GQ2/AdmissibleLimit.lean`; every theorem `#print axioms` = std-3; no allowlist changes вҖ”
  pure proof ticket).*  Deliverables: (i) `tameRelator_mem_NA`/`wildRelator_mem_NA` +
  `quotientMk_*Relator_eq_one` (relations (5)/(6) hold in `О“_A`); (ii) `wildCore` (the closed
  normal closure `вҹЁвҹЁxвӮҖ,xвӮҒвҹ©вҹ©`, on the raw quotient `FвӮ„ в§ё NA` вүЎбөҲбөүб¶  `GammaA`) with
  `isProP_wildCore : IsProP 2 wildCore`.  **P-05 interface**: `isAdmissibleU_iff_NA_le`
  (admissible opens = opens above `N_A`) and `generates_univMarking_map` (generation is automatic
  in every finite quotient вҖ” density of `FreeGroup` in its completion).  Engine (design note in
  the module docstring): `isAdmissibleU_top` (trivial quotient admissible вҖ” nonvacuity without
  App. B) + `isAdmissibleU_inf` (Lemma 2.1 subdirect closure, elementwise 2-power form
  `isPGroup_normalClosure_image_inf`) вҮ’ directedness вҮ’ compactness domination
  (`exists_isAdmissibleU_le`, the `proPKernel`-style argument) вҮ’ `isAdmissibleU_of_NA_le`
  (Lemma 2.2 pushforward).  Lean gotcha recorded: state `wildCore` on `FвӮ„ в§ё NA`, not
  `Subgroup GammaA` вҖ” mixing the `вҶҘGammaA` and raw-quotient spellings breaks instance search
  (`Membership`-instance mismatch), while everything is defeq on the raw type.
- **P-05** вҳ‘: the bijection `ContSurj GammaA G вүғ {t : Marking G // t.Admissible}` for finite discrete
  `G`: forward = push `univMarking` (admissible by P-04 + Lemma 2.2 `map_admissible`); backward =
  `quotientLift` along `NA_le_ker` (T-21); round-trips via `univMarking_map_toHom` and topological
  generation (P-03).  `Nat.card` conclusion in exactly `main_presentation`'s `hО“A` form.
  *Done (`GQ2/Prop23.lean`; zero sorries; `prop_2_3` and all helpers `#print axioms` = std-3).*
  Headline: `prop_2_3 : Nat.card (ContSurj GammaA G) = admissibleCount G` via
  `contSurjEquivAdmissible` (assembled from named halves `Marking.push`/`Marking.descend` with
  `push_admissible`, `descend_surjective`, `push_descend`, `descend_push`).  Key new lemma:
  `admissible_of_NA_le_ker` вҖ” the **converse of `NA_le_ker`** (surjective + `N_A вүӨ ker` вҮ’ pushed
  marking admissible, via P-04's `isAdmissibleU_of_NA_le` + Lemma 2.2 transfer along
  `quotientKerEquivOfSurjective`); together they characterize admissible markings of `G` as the
  continuous surjections `FвӮ„ вҶ  G` killing `N_A`.  **Deviations from this sketch**: (i) t.f.g.
  (P-03) is *not needed* вҖ” the round-trip uses the **uniqueness half of the universal property**
  (`Marking.toHom_univMarking_map`: every `f : FвӮ„ вҹ¶ P` is `toHom` of its own pushed marking;
  CMH-level form `toHom_hom_univMarking_map` via `ConcreteCategory.ofHom`, whose constructor is
  the public route вҖ” `ProfiniteGrp.Hom.mk` is private); (ii) the equiv is stated on `FвӮ„ в§ё NA`
  (defeq `GammaA`, the P-04 spelling convention), `prop_2_3` itself on `GammaA`.  Lean gotchas:
  prove uniqueness by `rw [Marking.toHom, Equiv.symm_apply_eq]` then rewrite
  `homEquiv_apply` **before** `fin_cases i <;> rfl` (otherwise `rfl` unfolds the completion
  adjunction вҖ” deterministic timeout), and keep the equiv's fields as *named* lemmas вҖ” inline
  `by`-blocks inside the `Equiv` literal retrigger the same timeout via nested-proof abstraction.

  failing; a tracked violation still FAILs (test, then delete the plant).  Gate: guard green on
  the current tree; the script diff reviewed against parallel allowlist edits (reconstruct from
  HEAD).
